***dunnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dunnen.html>dunnen</a> (49649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunnen.html>dunnen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dun.html>dun</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunnen.html>dunnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to thin, to become/make slender</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become/make sparse</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:durch.html>durch</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">duruh</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þurhw</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">through</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thorough</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">דורך</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durkh</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***durian.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:durian.html>durian</a> (83773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href = vnd.unilang:durian.html>durian</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Austronesian" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Austronesian">Proto-Austronesian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="map-pro">*duʀi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thorn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">iwi</i>, from Māori.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:durian.html>durian</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">durians</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several trees, genus <i>Durio</i>, of Southeast Asia.</li>
<li>The spiky edible fruit of this tree, known for its strong taste and very strong, unpleasant odor.
<ul><li><b>1692</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Boyle" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Boyle">Robert Boyle</a>, <i>General Heads for the Natural History of a Country Great or Small,</i> London: John <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a> and S. Hedford, “Enquiries for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Suratte" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dutch Suratte">Suratte</a>, amp;c.,” p. 96,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A28984.0001.001">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Whether the <i>Betele</i> hath such a contrariety to the <i><b>Durion</b></i>, that a few Leaves of that, put to a whole Shopful of <i><b>Durions</b></i>, will make them all <a href = vnd.unilang:rot.html>rot</a> suddenly; and whether those that have surfeited on <i><b>Durions</b></i>, and thereby over-heated themselves, do, by laying a Leaf or two of <i>Betele</i> upon their Breasts or Stomachs, immediately cure the Inflammations, and Recover.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1869</b> November,  “The <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>Land</a> of the Malay: A Record of Travel in the Oriental Tropics”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Mayne_Reid" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Mayne Reid">[Thomas] Mayne Reid</a>, editor, <cite>Onward: A Magazine for the Young Manhood of America</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  Onward Publishing Office, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/8717398">8717398</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=nQ7ZAAAAMAAJamp;pg=PA494">page 494</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a> I thoroughly enjoyed, for the various fruits of Singapore are delicious. One of them, the "<b>durion</b>," exhales a most noxious perfume, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> pleasant to the palate.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1956</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Burgess" class="extiw" title="w:Anthony Burgess">Anthony Burgess</a>,  <cite>Time for a Tiger</cite> (The Malayan Trilogy), published 1972, page 115:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Old women crouched <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bags.html>bags</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:siamese.html>Siamese</a> rice, skeps of red and green <a href = vnd.unilang:peppers.html>peppers</a>, purple egg-plants, bristly rambutans, pineapples, <b>durians</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A yellow colour, like that of <a href = vnd.unilang:durian.html>durian</a> flesh (also called <a href = vnd.unilang:durian.html>durian</a> yellow).
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:durian.html>durian</a> colour: <span style="background-color:E1BD27; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***durven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:durven.html>durven</a> (3244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:durven.html>durven</a></i>. This verb originated from two <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> verbs:
</p>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:durven.html>durven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to need</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thurvan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þurbaną</i>.</li>
<li><i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">durren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">durran</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*durzaną</i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:durven.html>durven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dare (do), to not be afraid (to do)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:durf.html>durf</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>dare</b> not <b>do</b> that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dare (to), to not be afraid to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:durfde.html>durfde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stap.html>stap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:autonoom.html>autonoom</a> natuurrecht <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoiets.html>zoiets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:impliceren.html>impliceren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaan.html>bestaan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>dared</b> not take the step towards an autonomous natural law, because by so doing it could be implied that <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> should not exist.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***dusdanig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dusdanig.html>dusdanig</a> (45584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dusdanich</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dusgedanich</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dusgedaen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thus done, made in such a way</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dusdanig.html>dusdanig</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>such</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zulk.html>zulk</a></span></li></ul>

***dutchman.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutchman.html>dutchman</a> (70279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutchman.html>Dutchman</a></i>. Attested mainly in the US from the late 19th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutchman.html>dutchman</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">dutchmen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">carpentry<span class="ib-comma">,</span> masonry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of wood or stone used to repair a larger piece, shaped such that it fills as exactly as possible a void or cavity that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to be repaired.</li>
<li>A flaw or void repaired with such a piece.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cloth strip attached to a <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> to conceal a joint.</li></ol>
</body>

***dutten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutten.html>dutten</a> (45581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. May be from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutten.html>dutten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, through the semantic development "rage"  |  "be out of one's mind"  |  "be unconscious"  |  "doze".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutten.html>dutten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to doze, to nap, to sleep lightly</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duur.html>duur</a> (1813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">diere</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dure.html>dure</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">diuri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*diurijaz</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i>.
</p>

***dwaas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a> (2543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dwaes</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dwās</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dwēsaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">quasseln</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwazer.html>dwazer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">dwaast</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foolish, stupid</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zot.html>zot</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwazen.html>dwazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">dwazin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a (male) stupid person, fool</li></ol>

***dwarrelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwarrelen.html>dwarrelen</a> (65328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dwerelen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*dweren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thweran</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þweraną</i>. The change in vowel from <i>e</i> to <i>a</i> may have happened by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warrelen.html>warrelen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarrelen.html>dwarrelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to whirl, to flutter</li></ol>

***dwars.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwars.html>dwars</a> (2191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dwers</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thwerhes</i>, genitive form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þwerhaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cross, adverse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thwart</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">queer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">tvär</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tvært</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:quer.html>quer</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌸𐍅𐌰𐌹𐍂𐌷𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">þwairhs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwars.html>dwars</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwars.html>dwarser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwars.html>dwars</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">dwarst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>in a crosswise direction, transverse, at right angles</li>
<li>slantwise, diagonal, askew</li>
<li>rebellious, stubbornly disobedient</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsbomen.html>dwarsboom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wooden crossbeam, wooden <a href = vnd.unilang:plank.html>plank</a> or pole placed horizontally</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsbomen.html>dwarsbomen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to thwart, frustrate, get in the way of <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">block or hamper a course of action</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsligger.html>dwarsligger</a> (76232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsliggen.html>dwarsliggen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsligger.html>dwarsligger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsliggers.html>dwarsliggers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsligger.html>dwarsliggertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An obstructor, a hinderer, an obstructionist <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncooperative and seeks to thwart something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdacht.html>verdacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsligger.html>dwarsligger</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ervan.html>ervan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:infiltrant.html>infiltrant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She suspected the <b>obstructionist</b> of being an infiltrator.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">dwarsdrijver</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A sleeper, a railroad tie.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsliggers.html>dwarsliggers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bleken.html>bleken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verrot.html>verrot</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A few of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sleepers.html>sleepers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> out to be <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">spoorbalk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">spoorbiels</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small book with its text aligned parallel to the spine.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:henk.html>Henk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dwarsliggers.html>dwarsliggers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:meegenomen.html>meegenomen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meertje.html>meertje</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:henk.html>Henk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> some <b>books with spine-parallel text</b> along to the lake.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dwerch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:dwerg.html>dwerg</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dwergaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">dwerch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zwerg</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dwarf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">dværg</i>.

***dwingen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwingen.html>dwingen</a> (3072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwingen.html>dwingen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thwingan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þwinganą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwingen.html>dwingen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force, coerce <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">someone</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forceren.html>forceren</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to constrain, enforce, cause inevitably</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to insist forcefully</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***dynamo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dynamo.html>dynamo</a> (40865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dynamo-electric machine</i>. The element <i>dynamo-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ultimately from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δύναμις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dúnamis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">power</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dynamo.html>dynamo</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">dynamos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An electricity generator, a dynamo-electric machine.</li>
<li>An energetic person.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">That new Vice President of Marketing <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a real <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dynamo.html>dynamo</a></b>; sales have already <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> up this quarter.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">energetic person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See also Thesaurus:doer</li></ul>

***earl.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>earl</a> (4463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">erle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">erl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">eorl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*erlaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">jarl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">erl</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*erōną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*arōną</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:jara.html>jara</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fight, battle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁er-</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orior</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rise, get up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄρνυμι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órnumi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to urge, incite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬆𐬭𐬆𐬥𐬀𐬊𐬌𐬙𐬌</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ərənaoiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">ऋणोति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṛṇóti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to arise, reach, move, attack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Also displaced unrelated but similar <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ealdorman</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:alderman.html>alderman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>earl</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:earls.html>earls</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nobility</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A British or Irish nobleman next in rank above a viscount and below a marquess; equivalent to a European count. A female using the style <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> termed a countess.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of various nymphalid butterflies of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Tanaecia" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Tanaecia"><i>Tanaecia</i></a></span>. Other butterflies in this genus are called counts and viscounts.</li></ol>
</body>
